| Field        | Value   |
|--------------|---------|
| Entrypoint   | 0x4D1C  |
| Data Size    | 2 bytes |
| Instructions | 2       |

```
      00 01 02 03 04 05 06 07  08 09 0A 0B 0C 0D 0E 0F
      -- -- -- -- -- -- -- --  -- -- -- -- -- -- -- --
4D10:                                      96 00                    ..  
```

#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x4D1C [0x96] UNSET_EVENT_NPC: Restore NPC after event (removes event NPC status)
  1: 0x4D1D [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```

### Event 65535.3

#### Metadata

| Field        | Value    |
|--------------|----------|
| Entrypoint   | 0x4D1E   |
| Data Size    | 13 bytes |
| Instructions | 3        |

```
      00 01 02 03 04 05 06 07  08 09 0A 0B 0C 0D 0E 0F
      -- -- -- -- -- -- -- --  -- -- -- -- -- -- -- --
4D10:                                            6E F8                n.
4D20: FF FF 7F F3 80 99 F8 FF  FF 7F 00                 ...........     
```

#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x4D1E [0x6E] EventEntity uses emote 38*
  1: 0x4D25 [0x99] Wait for EventEntity animation to complete
  2: 0x4D2A [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
